<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begeleiden.html>begeleiden</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.

***begraven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:begraven.html>begraven</a> (1317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">begrāven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bigravan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bigrabaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:graven.html>graven</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begraven.html>begraven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bury
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:begroef.html>begroef</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bot.html>bot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorganger.html>voorganger</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:begraven.html>begraven</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The dog <b>buried</b> his bone precisely where his predecessor <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>buried</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begraafplaats.html>begraafplaats</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrafenis.html>begrafenis</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begraven.html>begraven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">  past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begraven.html>begraven</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:begraven.html>begraven</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrijpen.html>begrijpen</a> (717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">begripen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bigrīpan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*bigrīpan</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grijpen.html>grijpen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrijpen.html>begrijpen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to understand (concepts, ideas), to comprehend</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The word does not mean "understand" in the sense of "to hear clearly". For this, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verstaan.html>verstaan</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used.

***begrip.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a> (3683)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bigrip</i>. Formed based on <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrijpen.html>begrijpen</a></i> from the original nominative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:greep.html>greep</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begripje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>understanding, comprehension
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiskunde.html>wiskunde</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I have no <b>comprehension</b> of mathematics.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> beyond my <b>comprehension</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onbegrip.html>onbegrip</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>understanding, empathy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vol.html>vol</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> full of <b>understanding</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>notion, concept, term
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verklaar.html>Verklaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:begrip.html>begrip</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Explain this <b>notion</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

***behagen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:behagen.html>behagen</a> (10887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:behagen.html>behagen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bihagon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bihagōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behagen.html>behagen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to delight, please, gratify</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behaaglijk.html>behaaglijk</a></span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:behandelen.html>behandelen</a> (2183)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:handelen.html>handelen</a></i>.

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to handle, to treat</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to deal with, address or discuss as a subject</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:behang.html>behang</a> (14274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behangen.html>behangen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>wallpaper
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behangpapier.html>behangpapier</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">behangselpapier</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:behartigen.html>behartigen</a> (37404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hart.html>hart</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-igen</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:behelp.html>behelp</a> (95415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">help</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">behelpe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to assist</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">beholpje</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">behelpen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make do</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">behelfen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to manage</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:behelp.html>behelp</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">behelps</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">behelping</b>, <i>simple past</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en">behelped</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaic, dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past-form-of" lang="en">beholp</b>, <i>past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">behelped</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaic, dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">beholpen</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To help (with); give aid or assistance to.

<dl><dd>But <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> live in a good hope of better times and then, hopefully, will this dessign be excuted; Meanwhile I must <b><a href = vnd.unilang:behelp.html>behelp</a></b> myself with this boock, so, as I have found it, and so as it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:behoefte.html>behoefte</a> (3334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoefte.html>behoefte</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeven.html>behoeven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoefte.html>behoefte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeftes.html>behoeftes</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeften.html>behoeften</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoefte.html>behoeftetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a need
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> bad <a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelukkig.html>gelukkig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorziet.html>voorziet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> apartement <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriendin.html>vriendin</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:behoefte.html>behoefte</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> have a bath at home, but fortunately my girlfriend's house meets that <b>need</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gisteravond.html>Gisteravond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opeens.html>opeens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongelofelijke.html>ongelofelijke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaas.html>kaas</a><b><a href = vnd.unilang:behoefte.html>behoefte</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fondue.html>fondue</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Yesterday evening I suddenly found myself with an urgent <b>need</b> for cheese, so I made some <a href = vnd.unilang:fondue.html>fondue</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> defecation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:behoefte.html>behoefte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You may defecate in the <a href = vnd.unilang:toilet.html>toilet</a> upstairs.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">behoeftich</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:behoeven.html>behoeven</a> (77187)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeven.html>behoeven</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bihuovon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bihōbōną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoeven.html>hoeven</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">behove</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be necessary for</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, obsolete <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">behufen</i> (cf. <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Behuf</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">behøve</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to need</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">behøve</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to need</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">behöva</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to have use for, to need</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeven.html>behoeven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to need

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:behoeven.html>behoeven</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitbreiden.html>uitbreiden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You can expand your house <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to <b>need</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:behoud.html>behoud</a> (13045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">behout</i>. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behouden.html>behouden</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:behoud.html>behoud</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>preservation, conserving, conservation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:behoud.html>behoud</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:taal.html>taal</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They stand up for the <b>preservation</b> of their language.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overheid.html>overheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strikte.html>strikte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:neutraliteit.html>neutraliteit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noodzakelijk.html>noodzakelijk</a> "<a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:behoud.html>behoud</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:welvaart.html>welvaart</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:des.html>des</a> lands <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:behoud.html>behoud</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrede.html>vrede</a>".</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The government saw strict neutrality as requisite "for the <b>preservation</b> and welfare of the country and for <b>preserving</b> the peace".</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> salvation
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heil.html>heil</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> conservatism, <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">less commonly</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> orthodoxy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:viel.html>viel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:goede.html>goede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aarde.html>aarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krachten.html>krachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:behoud.html>behoud</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not go down well among the forces of <b>conservatism</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***behouden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:behouden.html>behouden</a> (4011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:behouden.html>behouden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bihaldan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bihaldaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to keep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">be-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i>.

<ol><li>help, aid</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Expression: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:behulp.html>behulp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> with the aid of.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">baye</i>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">baie</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">baia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bāca</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:beide.html>beide</a> (1098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:beide.html>beide</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">beithe</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beide.html>beide</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>both</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used both with a noun, and on its own as a pronoun. However, when used as a pronoun to refer to two persons rather than <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> or animals, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beiden.html>beiden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often used instead.
